        SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Alt], [d].[BannerImageId], [d].[CreaDate], [d].[CreaUser], [d].[DocumentId], [d].[GalleryId], [d].[Guid], [d].[IsDeleted], [d].[IsStatus], [d].[Link], [d].[LoginCount], [d].[ModDate], [d].[ModUser], [d].[Name], [d].[OrderNo], [d].[PictureId], [d].[ThumbImageId], [d].[Title], [d].[Types], [d].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d]
        WHERE [d].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[ThumbImageId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Alt], [d0].[BannerImageId], [d0].[CreaDate], [d0].[CreaUser], [d0].[DocumentId], [d0].[GalleryId], [d0].[Guid], [d0].[IsDeleted], [d0].[IsStatus], [d0].[Link], [d0].[LoginCount], [d0].[ModDate], [d0].[ModUser], [d0].[Name], [d0].[OrderNo], [d0].[PictureId], [d0].[ThumbImageId], [d0].[Title], [d0].[Types], [d0].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d0]
        WHERE [d0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[PictureId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [d1].[Id], [d1].[Alt], [d1].[BannerImageId], [d1].[CreaDate], [d1].[CreaUser], [d1].[DocumentId], [d1].[GalleryId], [d1].[Guid], [d1].[IsDeleted], [d1].[IsStatus], [d1].[Link], [d1].[LoginCount], [d1].[ModDate], [d1].[ModUser], [d1].[Name], [d1].[OrderNo], [d1].[PictureId], [d1].[ThumbImageId], [d1].[Title], [d1].[Types], [d1].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d1]
        WHERE [d1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t2] ON [c].[Id] = [t2].[BannerImageId]
    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND ([c].[Id] = @__id_0)
) AS [t3]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d2]
    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [t3].[Id] = [t4].[DocumentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d3]
    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [t3].[Id] = [t5].[GalleryId]
ORDER BY [t3].[Id], [t3].[Id0], [t3].[Id1], [t3].[Id2], [t3].[Id3], [t4].[Id], [t5].[Id]"
